> The rules of this game are simple:
Guess the username of the next person to post, and (if you want to) predict how they will respond to your prediction of their response of your prediction.

[EDIT]
Every time you correctly guess the name of the next user, give yourself 2 points, if the name you guess starts with the same letter as the next user, give yourself one point!
The user with the most points when this thread closes wins!
[EDIT2]
Keep a track of who has how many points by placing a points=6 or something like it at the bottom of your reply!

```
#!/bin/bash
. /usr/lib/ubuntuforums/UF.sh
uf_login lkjoel
uf_load 1448287
uf_special --nextuser "compugeek32"
uf_dump
uf_post --force-yes
uf_unload

```

### Post by lkjoel on 2011-08-10
```
#include <ubuntuforums>
#include <iostream>
#include <string>

int main() {
  UF_Object *UF = new UbuntuForums();
  UF.setThread(1448287);
  UF.setType(UF_Type("game"));
  UF.setGame(UF_Game("nextuser"));
  UF.CalculateNextUser();
  if (UF.NextUser == UF_User(string("compugeek32"))) {
    std::cout << "compugeek32"
  }
}

```

Hey I worked hard making those, first I had to open them in Pitivi (lol Windows Live Video Editor doesn't like mkv and I know that Pitivi works fine with them), find the appropriate scene cut it out as precisely as I could, render them, then upload them to gifninja.com to have them converted to animated gifs, then fix them in Gimp after downloading them (it always messes up the dimensions), then crop them to the same dimensions, then upload them to imgur then post the image links here.

Linux, giving me the tools I need to post ponies everywhere.

function Init(){
	var uf = new UbuntuForums();

	var compy = uf.getUserByID(494510);
	var Silver_Fox_ = uf.getUserByID(611656);

	</script>
